ffmpeg -re -vsync auto -itsoffset 200ms -dump_attachment /tmp/dump.txt -vstats -frame_drop_threshold 1.0 -hex -qphist -hide_banner -xerror -copy_unknown -sn -start_at_zero -vn -benchmark -bitexact -dn -filter_threads 2  -y -i @@ -r 24 /tmp/test.avi
